    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[BrandId], [p].[BrandId1], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[Code], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[DatasheetPath], [p].[DescriptionEn], [p].[DescriptionVi], [p].[DisplayOrder], [p].[IsActive], [p].[IsFeatured], [p].[MachineTypeId], [p].[MachineTypeId1], [p].[NameEn], [p].[NameVi], [p].[ShortDescriptionEn], [p].[ShortDescriptionVi], [p].[SlugEn], [p].[SlugVi], [p].[TechnicalSpecsEn], [p].[TechnicalSpecsVi], [p].[UpdatedAt]

    WHERE [p].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit) AND (LOWER([p].[NameVi]) LIKE @__searchTerm_0_contains ESCAPE N'\' OR LOWER([p].[NameEn]) LIKE @__searchTerm_0_contains ESCAPE N'\' OR LOWER([p].[Code]) LIKE @__searchTerm_0_contains_1 ESCAPE N'\')
